style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: right 424.3pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>情形一：甲公司发行的债券有公开市场<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">当甲公司发行的债券有公开市场时，通常需考虑该债券的市场价格及市场利厚，因为其反映了甲公司的现有信用状况以及债权投资者所要求的现时回报率。甲公司结合其自身情况判断后认为，以自己发行的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券利率作为估计增量借款利率的起点最为恰当。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司在</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券利率的基础上，执行了如下步骤，以确定该租赁的增量借款利率：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第一步，确定</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券的市场利率。甲公司根据该债券的市场价格和剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的还款情况（即，每年末根据票面利率支付利息、到期一次性偿还本金），计算该债券的市场利率。该市场利率反映了甲公司的现有信用状况以及债权投资者所要求的现时回报率，甲公司无需因该债券的发行时间（即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年前）而进行额外调整。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第二步，调整借款金额的不同。</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券的金额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，租赁付款总额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。甲公司根据估计日市场情况考虑上述借款金额的不同是否影响借款利率并相应进行调整。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第三步，调整本息偿付方式的不同。该租赁是每年支付固定的租赁付款额，而</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券是每年末付息并到期一次性偿还本金。甲公司应考虑该事项对借款利率的影响并作相应调整。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第四步，调整借款期间的不同°该租赁的租赁期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，而</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券的剩余期间为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年。甲公司应考虑该事项对借款利率的影响并作相应调整。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第五步，调整抵押情况的不同。在确定增量借款利率时，租赁合同视为以租赁资产作为抵押而获得借款，而</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券无任何抵押。甲公司应考虑该事项对借款利率的影响并作相应调整。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>情形二：甲公司发行的债券没有公开市场<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>当甲公司发行的债券没有公开市场、但甲公司存在可观察的信用评级时，可考虑以与甲公司信用评级相同的企业所发行的公开交易的债豢利率为基础，确定上述第一步的参考利率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">当甲公司发行的债券没有公开市场、且甲公司没有可观察的信用评级时，在市场利率水平和甲公司信用状况在债券发行日至增量借款利率估计日期间没有发生重大变化的情况下，可考虑以该</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期债券发行时的实际利率为基础，作为估计增量借款利率的起点。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>确定参考利率后，将其调整为增量借款別率的步骤与情形一基本相同。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>情形三：甲公司没有任何借款<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>当甲公司没有任何借款时，可考虑通过银行询价的方式获取同期借款利率，并进行适当调整后确定其增量借款利率；或者，可考虑聘用第三方评级机构获取其信用评级，参考情形一下的方法确定其增量借款利率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 24pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（二）使用权资产的初始计量<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>使用权资产，是指承租人可在租赁期内使用租赁资产的权利。在租赁期开始日，承租人应当按照成本对使用权资产进行初始计量。该成本包括下列四项：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l40 level1 lfo37; tab-stops: 85.85pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁负债的初始计量金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l40 level1 lfo37; tab-stops: 85.85pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日或之前支付的租赁付款额；存在租赁激励的，应扣除已享受的租赁激励相关金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l40 level1 lfo37; tab-stops: 86.0pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人发生的初始直接费用。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l40 level1 lfo37; tab-stops: 87.2pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人为拆卸及移除租赁资产、复原租赁资产所在场地或将租赁资产恢复至租赁条款约定状态预计将发生的成本。前述成本属于为生产存货而发生的，适用《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——存货》。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">关于上述第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">项成本，承租人有可能在租赁期开始日就承担了上述成本的支付义务，也可能在特定期间内因使用标的资产而承担了相关义务。承租人应在其有义务承担上述成本时，将这些成本确认为使用权资产成本的一部分。但是，承租人由于在特定期间内将使用权资产用于生产存货而发生的上述成本，应按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——存货》进行会计处理。承租人应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——或有事项》对上述成本的支付义务进行确认和计量。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在某些情况下，承租人可能在租赁期开始前就发生了与标的资产相关的经济业务或事项。例如：租赁合同双方经协商在租赁合同中约定，标的资产需经建造或重新设计后方可供承租人使用；根据合同条款与条件，承租人需支付与资产建造或设计相关的成本。承租人如发生与标的资产建造或设计相关的成本，应适用其他相关准则(如《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——固定资产》)进行会计处理。同时，需要注意的是与标的资产建造或设计相关的成本不包括承租人为获取标的资产使用权而支付的款项，此类款项无论在何时支付,均属于租赁付款额。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>30</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司就某栋建筑物的某一层楼与出租人乙公司签订了为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁协议，并拥有</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的续租选择权。有关资料如下：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">初始租赁期内的不含税租金为每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，续租期间为每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>55000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，所有款项应于每年年初支付；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(2)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">为获得该项租赁，甲公司发生的初始直接费用为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，其中，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元为向该楼层前任租户支付的款项，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元为向促成此租赁交易的房地产中介支付的佣金；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(3)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">作为对甲公司的激励，乙公司同意补偿甲公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的佣金；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(4)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁期开始日，甲公司评估后认为，不能合理确定将行使续租选择权，因此，将租赁期确定为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年；（5）甲公司无法确定租赁内含利率，其增量借款利率为每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">该利率反映的是甲公司以类似抵押条件借入期限为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年、与使用权资产等值的相同币种的借款而必须支付的利率。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>为简化处理，假设不考虑相关税费影响。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>分析：承租人甲公司的会计处理如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第一步，计算租赁期开始日租贷付款额的现值，并确认租赁负债和使用权资产。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租贷期开始日，甲公司支付第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，并以剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年租金（每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）按</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">的年利率折现后的现值计量租赁负债。计算租赁付款额现值的过程如下：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">期租赁付款额=</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">50000</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">x9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">=450000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">租赁负债=剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">期租赁付款额的现值=</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">50000</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">5%,9）=355391</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">未确认融资费用=剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">期租赁付款额-剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">期租赁付款额的现值</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>=450000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>-355</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>391=94609</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（元）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>405391<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>租赁负债——未确认融资费用<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>94609<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：租赁负债--租赁付款额 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>450000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 60pt; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">银行存款（第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁付款额）50000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第二步，将初始直接费用计入使用权资产的初始成本。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：使用权资产 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 35pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：银行存款<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第三步，将已收的租赁激励相关金额从使用权资产入账价值中扣除。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：银行存款<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>5000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>5000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>综上，甲公司使用权资产的初始成本为：405391+20000-5000=420391（元）。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>（三）租赁负债的后续计量<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>1.计量基础<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日后，承租人应当按以下原则对租赁负债进行后续计量：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l25 level1 lfo38; tab-stops: 87.65pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>确认租赁负债的利息时，增加租赁负债的账面金额；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l25 level1 lfo38; tab-stops: 87.65pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>支付租赁付款额时，减少租赁负债的账面金额；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l25 level1 lfo38; tab-stops: 88.05pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>因重估或租赁变更等原因导致租赁付款额发生变动时，重新计量租赁负债的账面价值。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人应当按照固定的周期性利率计算租赁负债在租赁期内各期间的利息费用，并计入当期损益，但按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>17</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>借</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">款费用》等其他准则规定应当计入相关资产成本的，从其规定。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>此处的周期性利率，是指承租人对租赁负债进行初始计量时所采用的折现率，或者因租赁付款额发生变动或因租赁变更而需按照修订后的折现率对租赁负债进行重新计量时，承租人所采用的修订后的折现率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司与出租人乙公司签订了为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的商铺租赁合同。每年的租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>450000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，在每年年末支付。甲公司无法确定租赁内含利率，其增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5.04%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：在租赁期开始日，甲公司按租赁付款额的现值所确认的租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2600000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，甲公司向乙公司支付第一年的租赁付款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>450000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，其中，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>131040</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元(即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2600000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5.04%)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">是当年的利息，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>318960</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元(即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>450000-131</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>040)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">是本金，即租赁负债的账面价值减少</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>318960</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。甲公司的账务处理为：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：租赁负债——租赁付款额 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>450000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">贷：银行存款 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">450000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：财务费用——利息费用<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>131040</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：租赁负债——未确认融资费用<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>131040</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">未纳入租赁负债计量的可变租赁付款额，即，并非取决于指数或比率的可变租赁付款额，应当在实际发生时计入当期损益，但按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——存货</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">等其他准则规定应当计入相关资产成本的，从其规定。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>32</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】沿用[例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>31],</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">除固定付款额外，合同还规定租赁期间甲公司商铺当年销售额超过</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>OOOOOO</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的，当年应再支付按销售额的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">计算的租金，于当年年末支付。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 406.85pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：由于该可变租贷付款额与未来的销售额挂钩，而并非是取决于指数或比率的，因此不应被纳入租赁负债的初始计量中。假设在租赁的第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，该商铺的销售额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1500000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。甲公司第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末应支付的可变租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>30000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1500000x2%）,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在实际发生时计入当期损益，甲公司的账务处理为：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 406.85pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：营业成本（或销售费用） <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>30000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 366.2pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：银行存款等<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>30000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 406.85pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>2.租赁负债的重新计量<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 418.7pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日后，当发生下列四种情形时，承租人应当按照变动后的租赁付款额的现值重新计量租赁负债，并相应调整使用权资产的账面价值。使用权资产的账面价值已调减至零，但租赁负债仍需进一步调减的，承租人应当将剩余金额计入当期损益。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（1）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">实质固定付款额发生变动。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>如果租赁付款额最初是可变的，但在租赁期开始日后的某一时点转为固定，那么，在潜在可变性消除时，该付款额成为实质固定付款额，应纳人租赁负债的计量中。承租人应当按照变动后租赁付款额的现值重新计量租赁负债。在该情形下，承租人采用的折现率不变，即，采用租赁期开始日确定的折现率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>33</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司签订了一份为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的机器租赁合同。租金于每年年末支付，并按以下方式确定：第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，租金是可变的，根据该机器在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年下半年的实际产能确定；第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，每年的租金根据该机器在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年下半年的实际产能确定，即，租金将在第</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年耒榜变为固定付款额。在租赁期开始日，甲公司无法确定租赁内含利率，其増量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>5%<SUB>o</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">假设在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，根据该机器在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年下半年的实际产能所确定的租赁付款额为每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：本例中，在租赁期开始时，由于未来的租金尚不确定,因此甲公司的租赁负债为零。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，租金的潜在可变性消除，成为实质固定付款额（和每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元），因此甲公司应基于变动后的租赁付款额重新计量租赁负债，并釆用不变的折现率（即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">进行折现。在支付第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租金之后，甲公司后续年度需支付的租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>180000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>20000x9</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁付款额在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年末的现值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>142156</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元［即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>P/A,</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）］<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">未确认融资费用为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37844</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>180000-142156）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。甲公司在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年末的<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>相关账务处理如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>支付第一年租金：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：制造费用等<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 35pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：银行存款 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>确认使用权资产和租赁负债：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>142156</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁负债——未确认融资费用 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37844</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：租赁负债一租赁付款额 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>180000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（2）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">担保余值预计的应付金额发生变动。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁期开始日后，承租人应对其在担保余值下预计支付的金额进行估计。该金额发生变动的，承租人应当按照变动后租赁付款额的现值</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>重</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">新计量租赁负债。在该情形下，承租人采用的折现率不变。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>34</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】沿用（例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>27</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>］<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁期开始日后，承租人甲公司对该汽车在租赁期结束时的公允价值进行监测。假设在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，甲公司预计该汽车在租赁期结束时的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>30000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。那么，甲公司应将该担保余值下预计应付的金额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>40</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>000-30</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>000）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">纳入租赁付款额，并使用不变的折现率来重新计量租赁负债。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（3）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">用于确定租赁付款额的指数或比率发生变动。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 415.8pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日后、因浮动利率的变动而导致未来租赁付款额发生变动的，承租人应当按照变动后租赁付款额的现值重新计量租赁负债。在该情形下、承租人应采用反映利率变动的修订后的折现率进行折现。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 434.15pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日后.因用于确定租赁付款额的指数或比率（浮动利率除外）的变动而导致未来租赁付款额发生变动的，承租人应当按照变动后租赁付款额的现值重新计量租赁负债。在该情形下承租人采用的折现率不变。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>需要得注意的是，仅当现金流量发生变动时，即租赁付款额的变动生效时，承租人才应重新计量租赁负债，以反映变动后的租赁付款额。承租人应基于变动后的合同付款额，确定剩余租赁期内的租赁付款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>35</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】沿用［例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>24</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>］<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">假设在租赁第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初的消费者价格指数为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>135,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司在租赁期开始日采用的折现率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%<SUB>0</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，在对因消费者价格指数变化而导致未来租赁付款额的变动进行会计处理以及支付第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁付款额之前，租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>339320</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元［即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>50000+50000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,7）］</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。经消费者价格指数调整后的第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>54000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000x135X25）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：本例中，因用于确定租赁付款额的消费者价格指数的变动，而导致未来租赁付款额发生变动，甲公司应当于第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初重新计量租赁负债，以反映变动后的租赁付款额，即租赁负债应当以每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>54000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的租赁付款额（剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">笔）为基础进行重新计量。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，甲公司按以下金额重新计量租赁负债：每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>54000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的租赁付款额按不变的折现率（即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">进行折现，为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>366466</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元［即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>54000+54000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN>5%,7）］<EM><SUB>。</SUB></EM></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">因此，甲公司的租赁负债将增加</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>27146</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即重新计量后的租赁负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（366466</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）与重新计量前的租赁负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>339320</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）之间的差额。不考虑其他因素，甲公司相关账务处理如下。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>27146</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁负债——未确认融资费用<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4854</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：租赁负债——租赁付款额<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>32000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（4）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">购买选择权、续租选择权或终止租赁选择权的评估结果或实际行使情况发生变化。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁期开始日后，发生下列情形的，承租人应采用修订后的折现率对变动后的租赁付款额进行折现，以重新计量租赁负债：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l54 level1 lfo39; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>①</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>发生承租人可控范围内的重大事件或变化，且影响承租人是否合理确定将行使续租选择权或终止租赁选择权的，承租人应当对其是否合理确定将行使相应选择权进行重新评估。上述选择权的评估结果发生变化的，承租人应当根据新的评估结果重新确定租赁期和租赁付款额。前述选择权的实际行使情况与原评估结果不一致等导致租赁期变化的，也应当根据新的租赁期重新确定租赁付款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l54 level1 lfo39; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>②</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>发生承租人可疑影旳重大事件或变化，且影响承租人是否合理确定将行使购买选择权的，承租人应当对其是否合理确定将行使购买选择权进行重新评估。评估结果发生变化的，承租人应根据新的评估结果重新确定租赁付款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>上述两种情形下，承租人在计算变动后租赁付款额的现值时,应当采用剩余租赁期间的租赁内含利率作为折现率；无法确定剩余租赁期间的租赁内含利率的，应当采用重估日的承租人增量借款利率作为折现率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>36</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司与出租人乙公司签订了一份为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的设备租赁合同。甲公司计划开发自有设备以替代租赁资产，自有设备计划在</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年内投入使用。甲公司拥有在租赁期结束时以</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元购买该设备的选择权。每年的租赁付款额固定为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，于每年年末支付。甲公司无決确定租赁内今刊率、其増量借款利卒为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁开始日，甲公司对行使购买选择权的可能性进行评估后认为，不能合理确定将行使购买选择权。这是因为，甲公司计划开发自有设备，继而在租赁期结束时替代租贷资产。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：在租赁期开始日，甲公司确认的租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>43300</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元,即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>43</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>300=l0000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">%，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5）。租赁</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">负债将按以下方法摊销（如表</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">所示）：</SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">单位：元<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 20.95pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 80.4pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=107>
      <P class=ae

      style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'>x5%</SPAN></B><SPAN

    <TD

    width=114>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
      size=2><B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">③</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 20.95pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 88.45pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=118>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm"><FONT 
      size=2><B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">④</SPAN></B><B><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'>=</SPAN></B><B><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US

      size=2><B><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'>470</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 21.65pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 85.3pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=114>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
      size=2><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10000</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 21.65pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 88.45pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=ae

<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 119.0pt 136.5pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">注：为便于计算，本题中，年金现值系数取两位小数。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 47.25pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.5; tab-stops: 119.0pt 136.5pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">第5年的利息费用470</SPAN><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>=10000-9530</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p><FONT 
size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">假设在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，甲公司作出削减开发项目的战略决定，包搭上述替代设备的开发。该决定在甲公司的可控范围内，并影响其是否合理将行使购买选择权。甲公司预计该设备在租赁结束时的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。甲公司重新评估其行使购买选择权的可能性认为，其合理确定将行使该购买选择权。原因是：在租赁期结束时不大可能有可用的替代设备，并且该设备在租赁期结束时的预计市场价值</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）远高于行权价格</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）。因比，甲公司应在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末将购买选择权的行权价格纳入租贷付款额中。假设甲公司无法确定剩余租赁期间的租货内含利率，其第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末的增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5.5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，甲公司重新计量租赁负债以涵盖购买选择权的行权价格，并釆用修订后的折现率</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5.5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">进行折现。重新计量后的租赁负债(支付前</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的付款额后)为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>22960</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>22960=10</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>000x(P/F,</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5.5%,1)+(10000+5000)</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>P/F,</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5.5%,</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2)<SUB>o</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">此后，租赁负债将按表</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">所述方法进行后续计量：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 335.55pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">表</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">单位：元<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

    style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 19.9pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 92.95pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>14223</SPAN></B><SPAN

  <TR 
  style="HEIGHT: 22pt; mso-yfti-irow: 3; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes">
    <TD

      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>5</SPAN></I></B><SPAN

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 22pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 92.95pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=ae

      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>14223</SPAN></B><SPAN

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 22pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 91.9pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

      <P class=ae

      lang=EN-US 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>777*</SPAN></B><SPAN

    style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 22pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 94pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=125>
      <P class=ae
