      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>15000</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 22pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 96.45pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly" 
    width=129>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>—</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE></DIV>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">注：</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">第</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>5</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">年的利息费用</SPAN><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>777=10000+5000-14223</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">(行权价格)<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司租入一层办公楼，为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，并拥有可续租</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的选择权。初始租赁期间(即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年)的租赁付款额为每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，可选续租期间(即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年)的租赁付款额为每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>55000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，均在每年年初支付。在租赁期开始日，甲公司评估后认为，不能合理确定将会行使续租选择权，因此确定租赁期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年。甲公司无法确定租赁内含利率，其增量借款利車为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%<SUB>0</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁期开始日，甲公司支付第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁付款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，并确认租赁负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>355390</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>355390=50000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x(P/A,</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,9)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，甲公司的业务显著增长，其日益壮大的人员规模意味着需要扩租办公楼。为了最大限度降低成本，甲公司额外签订了一份为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年、在同一办公楼内其他楼层的租赁合同，在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初起租。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：将扩张的人员安置到在同一办公楼内其他楼层的决定，在甲公司的可控范围内，并影响其是否合理确定将行使现有租赁合同下的续租选择权。如果在其他办公楼中租入一个类似的楼层，甲公司可能会产生额外的费用，因为其人员将处于两栋不同的办公楼中、而将全部人员搬迁到其他办公楼的费用可能会更高。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末.甲公司主新评估</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>E</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">认为，其合理确定将行使现有租贷合同下的续租选择权，因此该租赁的租赁期由</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年变为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，在对租贷期的变化进行会计处理前，即基于</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年租赁期时，甲公司在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末的租赁负债（支付前</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的付款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>后）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>186160</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>186160=</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>50000+50000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，甲公司重新评估后的租贷期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，因此应将剰余租赁期（第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年）内的租赁付款额（共</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">笔）纳入租赁负债，并采用修订后的折现率进行折现。假设甲公司无法确定剩余租赁期间的租赁內含利率，其第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年末的增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4.5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。因此.甲公司重新计量后的租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>399030</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>399030=</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>50000+50000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4.5%,3）+55000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4.5%,5）</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/F</SPAN>，<SPAN lang=EN-US>4.</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>,3</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）<SUB><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>c</SPAN></SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>38</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司与出租人乙公司签订为期</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的库房租赁合同，每年年末支付固定租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。甲公司拥有在租赁期结束时以</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>300000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元购买该库房的选择权。在租赁期开始日，甲公司评估后认为，不能合理确定将行使该购买选择权。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，该库房所在地房价显著上涨，甲公司预计租赁期结束时该库房的市价为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>600000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，甲公司重新评估后认为，能够合理确定将行使该购买选择权。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：该库房所在地区的房价上涨属于市场情况发生的变化，不在甲公司的可控范围内。因此，虽然该事项导致购买选择权的评估结果发生变化，但甲公司不应在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末重新计量租赁负债。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">然而，如果甲公司在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末不可撤销地通知乙公司，其将在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年末行使购买选择权，则属于购买选择权实际行使情况发生了变化，甲公司需要在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末按修订后的折现率对变动后的租赁付款额进行折现，重新计量租赁负债。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>39</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司与出租人乙公司签订了一份办公楼租赁合同，每年的机赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元,于每年年末支付。甲公司无法确定租赁内含利率，其增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>5%<SUB>o</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">不可撤销租赁期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，并且合同约定在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，甲公司有权选择以每年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元续租</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，也有权选择以</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元购买该房产。甲公司在租赁期开始时评估认为，可以合理确定将行使续租选择权，而不会行使购买选择权，因此将租赁期确定为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：在租赁期开始日，甲公司确认的租赁负债和使用权资产为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>386000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x(P/A,</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,10)=386000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(元)。租赁负债将按表</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">所述方法进行后续计量：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 355.1pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
表</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">单位：元<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

  <TR style="HEIGHT: 19.9pt; mso-yfti-irow: 2; mso-height-rule: exactly">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 19.9pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 51.05pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=68>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
      size=2><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 19.9pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 90.5pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt"

style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">注;</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">*</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">为便于计算，本題中,年金现值系数取两位小数。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p><FONT 
size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日，甲公司的账务处理为：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>386000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁负债——未确认融资费用<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">(500000-386000)<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">114000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 36.6pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.66"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：租赁负债一租赁付款额<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>500000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，该房产所在地房价显著上涨，甲公司预计租贷期结束时该房产的市价为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，甲公司在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末重新评估后认为，能够合理确定将行使上述购买选择权，而不会行使上述续租选择权：该房产所在地区的房价上涨属于市场情况发生的变化，不在甲公司的可控范围内。因此，虽然该事项导致购买选择权及续租选择权的评估结果发生变化，但甲公司不需重新计量租赁负债。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年末、甲公司实际行使了购买选择权。截至该时点，使用权资产的原值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>386000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，累计折旧为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>193000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>386000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5/10）</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">支付了第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年租赁付款额之后，租赁负债的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>216490</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，其中，租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>250000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，未确认融资费用为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>33510</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>250000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>-216</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>490）。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司行使购买选择权的会计分录为：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：固定资产——办公楼 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN>976<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN>510<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>使用权资产累计折旧 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN>193<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN>000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>租赁负债——租赁付款额<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>250<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN>000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>386000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>租赁负债——未确认融资费用<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>33510<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>银行存款<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN>1000000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>（四）使用权资产的后续计量<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>1.计量基础<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日后，承租人应当采用成本模式对使用权资产进行后续计量，即，以成本减累计折旧及累计减值损失计量使用权资产。I<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人按照本准则有关规定重新计量租赁负债的，应当相应调整使用权资产的账面价值。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">.使用权资产的折旧<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人应当参照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——固定资产》有关折旧规定，自租赁期开始日起对使用权资产计提折旧。使用权资产通常应自租赁期开始的当月计提折旧，当月计提确有困难的，为便干实务操作，企业也可以选择自租赁期开始的下月计提折旧，但应对同类使用权资产采取相同的折旧政策。计提的折旧金额应根据使用权资产的用途，计入相关资产的成本或者当期损益。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人在确定使用权资产的折旧方法时，应当根据与使用权资产有关的经济利益的预期实现方式做岀决定。通常，承租人按直线法对使用权资产计提折旧，其他折旧方法更能反映使用权资产有关经济利益预期实现方式的，应采用其他折旧方法。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人在确定使用权资产的折旧年限时，应遵循以下原则：承租人能够合理确定租赁期届满时取得租赁资产所有权的，应当在租赁资产剩余使用寿命内计提折旧；承租人无法合理确定租赁期届满时能够取得租赁资产所有权的，应当在租赁期与租赁资产剩余使用寿命两者孰短的期间内计提折旧。如果使用权资产的剩余使用寿命短于前两者，则应在使用权资产的剩余使用寿命内计提折旧。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>3.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">使用权资产的减值<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁期开始日后，承租人应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——资产减值》的规定，确定使用权资产是否发生减值，并对已识别的减值损失进行会计处理。使用权资产发生减值的，按应减记的金额,借记“资产减值损失”科目，贷记“使用权资产减值准备”科目。使用权资产减值准备一旦计提，不得转回。承租人应当按照扣除减值损失之后的使用权资产的账面价值，进行后续折旧。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>40</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司签订了一份为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的机器租赁合同，用于甲公司生产经营。相关使用权资产的初始账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，按直线法在</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年内计提折旧，年折旧费为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年末，确认该使用杖资产发生的减值损失</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，计入当期损益。该使用权责产在减值前账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>100000x5/</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。计提减值损失之后，该使用权资产的账而价值减至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>30000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>-</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000）,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">之后每年的折旧费也相应减至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>30000/5</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 405.6pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">企业执行本准则后.《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——或有事项》有关亏损合同的规定便适用于采用短期租赁和低价值资产租赁简化处理方法的租赁合同以及在租赁开始日前已是亏损合同的租赁合同，不再适用于其他租赁合同。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（五）租赁变更的会计处理<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁变更，是指原合同条款之外的租赁范围、租赁对价、租赁期限的变更，包括增加或终止一项或多项租赁资产的使用权，延长或缩短合同规定的租赁期等。租赁变更生效日，是指双方就租赁变更达成一致的日期。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁变更作为一项单独租赁处理<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁发生变更且同时符合下列条件的，承租人应当将该租赁变更作为一项单独租赁进行会计处理：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（1）<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">该租赁变更通过增加一项或多项租赁资产的使用权而扩大了租赁范围或延长了租赁期限；<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（2）<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">增加的对价与租赁范围扩大部分或租赁期限延长部分的单独价格按该合同情况调整后的金额相当。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">［</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>41</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">］</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人甲公司与出租人乙公司就</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米的办公场所签订了一项为期1</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁合同。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，甲公司和乙公司同意对原租赁合同进行变更，以扩租同一办公楼内</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米的办公场所。扩租的场所于第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年第二季度末可供甲公司使用。增加的租赁对价与新增</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米办公场所的当前市价（根据甲公司获取的扩租折扣进行调整后的金额）相当。扩租折扣反映了乙公司节约的成本，即，若将相同场所租贷给新租户，乙公司将会发生的额外成本（如营销成本）。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：在本例中，甲公司应当将该变更作为一项单独的租赁，与原来的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期租贷分别进行会计处理：原因在于，该租赁变更通过增加</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米办公场所的使用权而扩大了租赁范</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>围,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">并且增加的租赁对价与新增使用权的单独价格按该合同情况调整后的金额相当。据此，在新租赁的租赁期开始日（即第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年第二季度末），甲公司确认与新增</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米办公场所租贷相关的使用权资产和租赁负债。甲公司对原有</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方来办公场所租赁的会计处理不会因为该租赁变更而进行任何调整。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l51 level1 lfo40"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">1.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁变更未作为一项单独租赁处理<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁变更未作为一项单独租赁进行会计处理的，在租赁变更生效日，承租人应当按照本准则有关租赁分拆的规定对变更后合同的对价进行分摊；按照本准则有关租赁期的规定确定变更后的租赁期；并采用变更后的折现率对变更后的租赁付款额进行折现，以重新计量租赁负债。在计算变更后租赁付款额的现值时，承租人应当采用剩余租赁期间的租赁内含利率作为折现率；无法确定剩余租赁期间的租赁内含利率的，应当采用租赁变更生效日的承租人增量借款利率作为折现率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>就上述租赁负债调整的影响、承租人应区分以下情形进行会计处理：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（1）<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁变更导致租赁范围缩小或租赁期缩短的，承租人应当调减使用权资产的账面价值，以反映租赁的部分终止或完全终止。承租人应将部分终止或完全终止租赁的相关利得或损失计入当期损益。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（2）<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">其他租赁变更，承租人应当相应调整使用权资产的账面价值。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 385.45pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>42】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人甲公司与出租人乙公司就</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米的办公场所签订了</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期的租赁合同。年租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，在每年年末支付。甲公司无法确定租赁内含利率。在租赁期开始日，甲公司的増量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">相应的租赁负债和使用权资产的初始确认金额均为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>736000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>736000=100000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6%,10）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初、甲公司和乙公司同意对原租赁合同进行变更，即自第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初起，将原租赁场所缩减至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2500</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米。每年的租赁付款额（自第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年）调整为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>60000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。承租人在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初的增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 410.95pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：在租赁变更生效日（即第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初），甲公司基于以下情况对租赁负债进行重新计量：①剩余租赁期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年；②年付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>60000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；③采用修订后的折现率</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">进行折现。据此，计算得出租赁交更后的租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>259770</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>259770=60000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司应基于原使用权资产部分终止的比例（即缩减的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2500</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米占原使用权资产的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50%）,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">来确定使用权资产账面价值的调减金额。在租赁变更之前，原使用权资产的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>368000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>736000x5/10</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>184000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；原租赁负债的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>421240</SPAN><I><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元</SPAN></I><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">［即，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>100000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6%,</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）］<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">的账面价值为力21</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0620</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。因此，在租赁变更生效日（第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初），甲公司终止确认<I>50%</I>的原使用权资产和原租赁负债，并将租赁负债减少额与使用权资产减少额之间的差额<I>26620</I>元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>210620-184000</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">作为利得计入当期损益。其中，租赁负债的减少额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（210620</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）包括：租贷付款额的减少额250000元（即，100000x50%x5）,以及未确认融资费用的减少额39380元（即，250000-210620）。甲公司终止确认50%的原使用权资产和原租赁负债的账务处理为：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: major-fareast"><FONT 
size=3>借：租赁负债——租赁付款额<SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
</SPAN>250000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: major-fareast"><FONT 
size=3>贷：租赁负债——未确认融资费用 39380<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: major-fareast"><FONT 
size=3>使用权资产 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>184000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: major-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: major-fareast"><FONT 
size=3>资产处置损益<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>26629<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">此外，甲公司将剩余租赁负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（210620</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）与变更后重新计量的租赁负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>259770</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）之间的差额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>49150</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，相应调整使用权资产的账面价值。其中，租赁负债的增加额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>49150</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）包括两部分：租赁付款额的增加额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元[即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>60000-100000*50%）</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x5],</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">以及未确认融资费用的增加额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>850</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>-49</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>150</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）<SUB><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>o</SPAN></SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司调整现使用权资产价值的账务处理为：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>49150</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 30pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁负债——未确认融资费用<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>850</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 35pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：租赁负债一租赁付款额<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU"><FONT 
size=3>注：100000x（P/A,6%,10）=736010（元），为便于计算，本题中，作尾数调整，取736000元。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>43</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司与出租人乙公司就</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米的办公场所签订了一项为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁。年租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，在每年年末支付。甲公司无法确定租赁内含利率。甲公司在租赁期开始日的增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>6%<SUB>。</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，甲公司和乙公司同意对原租赁合同进行变更，即，将租赁期延长</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年。每年的租赁付款额不变（即在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>14</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的每年年末支付</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）。甲公司在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初的增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7%<SUB>。</SUB></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：在租贷变更生效日（即第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初），甲公司基于下列情况对租赁负债进行重新计量：①剩余租赁期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年；②年付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；③采用修订后的折现率</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">进行折现。据此，计算得出租赁变更后的租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>597130</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>597130=100000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>P/A</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>,7%,</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）<SUB>。</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租货变更前的租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>346510</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元,即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>346510=100000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6%,</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司将变更后租赁负债的账面价值与变更前的账面价值之间的差额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>250620</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>597</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>130-346510</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">相应调整使用权资产的账面价值。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（六）短期租赁和低价值资产租赁<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则规定、对于短期租赁和低价值资产租赁，承租人可以选择不确认使用权资产和租赁负债。作岀该选择的，承租人应当将短期租赁和低价值资产租赁的租赁付款额，在租赁期内各个期间按照直线法或其他系统合理的方法计入相关资产成本或当期损益。其他系统合理的方法能够更好地反映承租人的受益模式的，承租人应当采用该方法。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">短期租赁<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">本准则规定，短期租赁，是指在租赁期开始日，租赁期不超过</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月的租赁。包含购买选择权的租赁不属于短期租赁。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对于短期租赁，承租人可以按照租赁资产的类别作出采用简化会计处理的选择。如果承租对某类租赁资产作出了简化会计处理的选择，未来该类资产下所有的短期租赁都应采用简化会计处理。某类租赁资产是指企业运营中具有类似性质和用途的一组租赁资产。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 404.7pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>按照简化会计处理的短期租赁发生租赁变更或者其他原因导致租赁期发生变化的，承租人应当将其视为一项新租赁，重新按照上述原则判断该项新租赁是否可以选择简化会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>44</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人与出租人签订了一份租赁合同，约定不可撤销期间为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月，且承租人拥有</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月的续租选择权。在租赁期开始日，承租人判断可以合理确定将行使续租选择权，因为续租期的月租赁付款额明显低于市场价格。在此情况下，承租人确定租赁期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月，不属于短期租赁，承租人不能选择上述简化会计处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">低价值资产租赁<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>低价值资产租赁，是指单项租赁资产为全新资产时价值较低的租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人在判断是否是低价值资产租赁时，应基于租赁资产的全新状态下的价值进行评估，不应考虑资产已被使用的年限。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对于低价值资产租赁，承租人可根据每项租赁的具体情况作岀简化会计处理选择。低价值资产同时还应满足本准则第十条的规定，即，只有承租人能够从单独使用该低价值资产或将其与承租人易于获得的其他资源一起使用中获利，且该项资产与其他租赁资产没有高度依赖或高度关联关系时，才能对该资产租赁选择进行简化会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>低价值资产租赁的标准应该是一个绝对金额，即仅与资产全新状态下的绝对价值有关，不受承租人规模、性质等影响，也不考虑该资产对于承租人或相关租赁交易的重要性。常见的低价值资产的例子包括平板电脑、普通办公家具、电话等小型资产。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>但是，如果承租人已经或者预期要把相关资产进行转租赁，则不能将原租赁按照低价值资产租赁进行简化会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>值得注意的是，符合低价值资产租赁的，也并不代表承租人若采取购入方式取得该资产时该资产不符合固定资产确认条件。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>45</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人与出租人签订了一份租赁合同，约定的租赁资产包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(1)</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>IT</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">设备，包括供员工个人使用的笔记本电脑、台式电脑、平板电脑、桌面打印机和手机等；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">服务器，其中包括增加服务器容量的单独组件，这些组件根据承租人需要陆续添加到大型服务器以增加服务器存储容量；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">办公家具，如桌椅和办公隔断等；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(4)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">饮水机。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">通常，办公笔记本电脑全新时的单独价格不超过人民币</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，台式电脑、平板电脑、桌面打印机和手机全新时的单独价格不超过人民币</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">兄，普通办公家具的单独价格不超过人民币</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，饮水机的单独价格不超过人民币</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，服务器单个组件单独价格不超过人民币</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：上述租赁资产中，各种IT设备、办公家具、饮水机都够单独使承租人获益</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">且与其他租赁资产没有高度依赖或高度关联关系。通常情况下，符合低价值资产租赁的资产全新状态下的绝对价值应低于人民币</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>40000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。本例中，承租人将</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>1T</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">设备、办公具、饮水机作为低价值租赁资产，选择按照简化方法进行会计处理。对于服务器中的组件，尽管单个组件的单独价格较低，但由于每组件都与服务器中的其他部分高度相关，承租人若不租赁服务器不会租赁这些组件，构成单独的租赁部分，因此不能作为低价租赁资产进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20.1pt; mso-outline-level: 2; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_Toc72425524><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>八、出租人会计处理</FONT></SPAN></B></A><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（一）出租人的租赁分类<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo41"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">1.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>融资租赁和经营租赁<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则规定，出租人应当在租赁开始日将租赁分为融资租赁和经营租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁开始日，是指租赁合同签署日与租赁各方就主要租赁条款作出承诺日中的较早者。租赁开始日可能早于租赁期开始日，也可能与租赁期开始日重合。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>一项租赁属于融资租赁还是经营租赁取决于交易的实质，而不是合同的形式。如果一项租赁实质上转移了与租赁资产所有权有关的几乎全部风险和报酬，出租人应当将该项租赁分类为融资租赁。出租人应当将除融资租赁以外的其他租赁分类为经营租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在本准则中，岀租人的租赁分类是以租赁转移与租赁资产所有权相关的风险和报酬的程度为依据的。风险包括由于生产能力的闲置或技术陈旧可能造成的损失，以及由于经济状况的改变可能造成的回报变动。报酬可以表现为在租赁资产的预期经济寿命期间经营的盈利以及因增值或残值变现可能产生的利得。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁开始日后，除非发生租赁变更，出租人无需对租赁的分类进行重新评估。租赁资产预计使用寿命、预计余值等会计估计变更或发生承租人违约等情况变化的，出租人不对租赁进行重分类。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁合同可能包括因租赁开始日与租赁期开始日之间发生的特定变化而需对租赁付款额进行调整的条款与条件（例如，岀租人标的资产的成本发生变动，或出租人对该租赁的融资成本发生变动）。在此情况下，出于租赁分类目的，此类变动的影响均视为在租赁开始日已发生。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo41"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">2.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>融资租赁的分类标准<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>一项租赁存在下列一种或多种情形的，通常分类为融资租赁：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo42; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期届满时，租赁资产的所有权转移给承租人。即，如果在租赁协议中已经约定、或者根据其他条件，在租赁开始日就可以合理地判断、租赁期届满肘出租人会将资产的所有权转移给承租人.那么该项租赁通常分类为融资租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo42; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人有购买租赁资产的选择权，所订立的购买价款预计将远低于行使选择权时租赁资产的公允价值，因而在租赁开始日就可以合理确定承租人将行使该选择权。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo42; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">资产的所有权虽然不转移、但租赁期占租赁资产使用寿命的大部分：实务中，这里的“大部分”一般指租赁期占租赁开始日租赁资产使用寿命的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>75%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">以上(含</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>75%</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>)<SUB>o</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">需要说明的是，这里的量化标准只是指导性标准，企业在具体运用时，必须以准则规定的相关条件进行综合判断，这条标准强调的是租赁期占租赁资产使用寿命的比例，而非租赁期占该项资产全部可使用年限的比例。如果租赁资产是旧资产，在租赁前已使用年限超过资产自全新时起算可使用年限的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>75%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">以上时，则这条判断标准不适用，不能使用这条标准确定租赁的分类。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo42"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁开始日，租赁收款额的现值几乎相当于租赁资产的公允价值。实务中，这里的“几乎相当于”，通常掌握在</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>90%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">以上。需要说明的是，这里的量化标准只是指导性标准，企业在具体运用时，必须以准则规定的相关条件进行综合判断。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo42"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(5)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁资产性质特殊，如果不作较大改造，只有承租人才能使用。租赁资产由岀租人根据承租人对资产型号、规格等方面的特殊要求专门购买或建造的，具有专购、专用性质。这些租赁资产如果不作较大的重新改制，其他企业通常难以使用。这种情况下，通常也分类为融资租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>一项租赁存在下列一项或多项迹象的，也可能分类为融资租赁：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l61 level1 lfo43; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>若承租人撤销租赁，撤销租赁对出租人造成的损失由承租人承担。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l61 level1 lfo43; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>资产余值的公允价值波动所产生的利得或损失归属于承租人。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>例如，租赁结束时，出租人以相当于资产销售收益的绝大部分金额作为对租金的退还，说明承租人承担了租赁资产余值的几乎所有风险和报酬。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l61 level1 lfo43; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人有能力以远低于市场水平的租金继续租赁至下一期间。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>此经济激励政策与购买选择权类似，如果续租选择权行权价远低于市场水平，可以合理确定承租人将继续租赁至下一期间。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>值得注意的是，岀租人判断租赁类型时，上述情形和迹象并非总是决定性的，而是应综合考虑经济激励的有利方面和不利方面。若有其他特征充分表明，租赁实质上没有转移与租赁资产所有权相关的几乎全部风险和报酬，则该租赁应分类为经营租赁。例如，若租赁资产的所有权在租赁期结束时是以相当于届时其公允价值的可变付款额转让至承租人，或者因存在可变租赁付款额导致出租人实质上没有转移几乎全部风险和报酬，就可能岀现这种情况。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 24.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（二）出租人对融资租赁的会计处理<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l33 level1 lfo44"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">1. </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>初始计量<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则规定，在租赁期开始日，出租人应当对融资租赁确认应收融资租赁款，并终止确认融资租赁资产。出租人对应收融资租赁款进行初始计量时，应当以租赁投资净额作为应收融资租赁款的入账价值。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 413.45pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁投资净额为未担保余值和租赁期开始日尚未收到的租赁收款额按照租赁内含利率折现的现值之和。租赁内含利率，是指使出租人的租赁收款额的现值与未担保余值的现值之和(即租赁投资净额)等于租赁资产公允价值与出租人的初始直接费用之和的利率。因此，出租人发生的初始直接费用包括在租赁投资净额中，也即包括在应收融资租赁款的初始入账价值中。<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #bfa89d; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 413.45pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: #bfa89d; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'></SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁收款额，是指岀租人因让渡在租赁期内使用租赁资产的权利而应向承租人收取的款项，包括：</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 413.45pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人需支付的固定付款额及实质固定付款额。存在租赁激励的，应当扣除租赁激励相关金额。</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 413.45pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>取决于指数或比率的可变租赁付款额。该款项在初始计/时根据租赁期开始日的指数或比率确定。</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 413.45pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">购买选择权的行权价格，前提是合理确定承租人将行使该选择权</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l19 level1 lfo45; tab-stops: 86.75pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人行使终止租赁选择权需支付的款项，前提是租赁期反映岀承租人将行使终止租赁选择权。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l19 level1 lfo45; tab-stops: 86.6pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(5) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>由承租人、与承租人有关的一方以及有经济能力履行担保义务的独立第三方向岀租人提供的担保余值。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>46</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日，甲公司与乙公司签订了一份租赁合同，从乙公司租入塑钢机一台。租赁合同主要条款如下：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 86.2pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁资产：全新塑钢机。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 86.2pt"><SPAN
