style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁期开始日：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x20</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日。</SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 86.2pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"></SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>(3)</FONT> </SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">租赁期：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">2x20</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">日</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">一</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">2x25</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">日，共</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">72个月。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 86.2pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">固定租金支付：自</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x20</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日，每年年末支付租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>I160000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。如果甲公司能够在每年年末的最后一天及时付款，则给予减少租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的奖励。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 86.2pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(5) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>取决于指数或比率的可变租赁付款额：租赁期限内，如遇中国人民银行贷款基准利率调整时，出租人将对租赁利率作出同方向、同幅度的调整。基准利率调整日之前各期和调整日当期租金不变，从下一期租金开始按调整后的租金金额收取。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 89.0pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(6) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁开始日租赁资产的公允价值：该机器在</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>700000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>600000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 89.0pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(7) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">初始直接费用：签订租赁合同过程中乙公司发生可归属于租赁项目的手续费、佣金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 89.0pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(8) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人的购买选择权：租赁期届满时，甲公司享有优惠购买该机器的选择权，购买价为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，估计该日租赁资产的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>80000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 89.0pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(9) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">取决于租赁资产绩效的可变租赁付款额：</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x21</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年和</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年两年，甲公司每年按该机器所生产的产品一塑钢窗户的年销售收入的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">向乙公司支付。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 93.15pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(10) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人的终止租赁选择权：甲公司享有终止租赁选择权。在租赁期间，如果甲公司终止租赁，需支付的款项为剩余租赁期间的固定租金支付金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 92.5pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(11) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">担保余值和未担保余值均为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l64 level1 lfo46; tab-stops: 92.7pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(12) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">全新塑钢机的使用寿命为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>分析：出租人乙公司的会计处理如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第一步，判断租赁类型。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">本例存在优惠购买选择权，优惠购买价</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元远低于行使选择权日租赁资产的公允价值</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>80000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，因此在</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日就可合理确定甲公司将会行使这种选择权。另外，在本例中，租赁期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，占租赁开始日租赁资产使用寿命的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>86%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(占租赁资产使用寿命的大部分)。同时，乙公司综合考虑其他各种情形和迹象，认为该租赁实质上转移了与该项设备所有权有关的几乎全部风险和报酬，因此将这项租赁认定为融资租赁。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第二步，确定租赁收款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(1)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人的固宅付款额为考虑扣除租贷激励后的金额。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(160</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: EN-US">000-10000)x6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">=900000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">(元)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l50 level1 lfo47; tab-stops: 29.55pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>取决于指数或比率的可变租贷付款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>该款项在初始计量时根据租赁期开始日的指数或比率确定，因此本例題在租赁期开是日不做考虑。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l50 level1 lfo47; tab-stops: 121.35pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人购买选择权的行权价格。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁期届满时，甲公司享有优惠购买该机器的选择权，购习价格为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，估计该日租赁资产的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>80000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。优惠价</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元远低于行使选择权日租赁资产的公允价值，因此在</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日就可合理确定甲公司将会行使这种选择权。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">结论：租赁付款额中应包括承租人购买选择权的行权</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l50 level1 lfo47; tab-stops: 121.35pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>终止租赁的罚款。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>虽然甲公司享有终止租赁选择权，但若终止租赁，甲公司付的款项为剩余租赁期间的固定租金支付金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>结论：根据上述条款，可以合理确定甲公司不会行使终止选择权<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l50 level1 lfo47; tab-stops: 121.35pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(5) </SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">由承租人向出租人提供的担保余值：甲公司向乙公司提供的担保余值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">综上所述租赁收款额为：</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">900000+20000=920000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">(元)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第三步，确认租赁投资总额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁投资总额=在融资租赁下出租人应收的租赁收款额+未保余值<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">本例中租赁投资总额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">=920000+0=920000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">(元)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第四步，确认租赁投资净额的金额和未实现触资收益<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁投资净额在金额上等于机赁资产击租赁期开始日公允价值</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>700000+</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">出租人发生的租赁初始直樓费用</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>000=710000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（元）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">未实现融资收益=租赁投资总额-租赁投资净额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">=920000-710000=210000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第五步，计算租赁内含利率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁内含利率是使租赁投资总额的现值（即租赁投资净额）等于租赁资产在租赁开始日的公允价值与出租人的初始直接费用之和的利率。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">本例中列出公式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">150000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,r,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">6）</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">+20000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/F,r,6</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US>=710000</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元），计算得到租赁的内含利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">7.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">82%<SUB>0</SUB><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第六步，账务处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x20</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：应收融资租赁款一租赁收款额 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>920000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 35pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：银行存款10000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 55pt; mso-char-indent-count: 5.5"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>融资租赁资产600000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 55pt; mso-char-indent-count: 5.5"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>资产处置损益100000</FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 55pt; mso-char-indent-count: 5.5"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">应收融资租赁款——未实现融资收益<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>210000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>若某融资租赁合同必须以收到租赁保证金为生效条件，出租人收到承租人交来的租赁保证金，借记“银行存款”科目，贷记“其他应收款一租赁保证金”科目。承租人到期不交租金，以保证金抵作租金时，借记“其他应收款一租赁保证金”科目，贷记“应收融资租赁款”科目。承租人违约，按租赁合同或协议规定没收保证金时，借记“其他应收款——租赁保证金”科目，贷记“营业外收入”等科目。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l33 level1 lfo44"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">2. </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>融资租赁的后续计量<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 23pt auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">出租人应当按照固定的周期性利率计算并确认租赁期内各个期间的利息收入。该周期性利率，是按照本准则第三十八条规定所采</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">用的折现率，或者按照木准则第四十四条规定所采用的修订后的折现率。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ac 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=2><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>47</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】沿用［例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>46</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>］</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">以下说明出租人如何确认计量租赁期內各期间的利息收入。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ac 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: right 434.45pt"><FONT 
size=2><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ac 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: right 434.45pt"><FONT 
size=2><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"></SPAN></SPAN></FONT><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第一步、计算租赁期内#期的利息收入（如表</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">所示）。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 321.55pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">表</SPAN><B><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'>5<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">单位：元<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

size=3><SPAN

style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-language: ZH-CN'>48134</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 269.0pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p><FONT size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则规定，纳入出租人租赁投资净额的可变租赁付款额只包含取决于指数或比率的可变租赁付款额。在初始计量时，应当采用租赁期开始日的指数或比率进行初始计量。出租人应定期复核计算租赁投资总额时所使用的未担保余值。若预计未担保余值降低，岀租人应修改租赁期内的收益分配，并立即确认预计的减少额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人取得的未纳入租赁投资净额计量的可变租赁付款额，如与资产的未来绩效或使用情况挂钩的可变租赁付款额，应当在实际发生时计入当期损益。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>48</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】沿用【例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>46</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>】<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">假设</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x21</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年和</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，甲公司分别实现塑钢窗户年销售收入</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">和</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1500000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。根据租赁合同，乙公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x21</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年和</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年应向甲公司收取的与销售收入挂钩的租金分别为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元和</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>75000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>分析：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>会计分录为：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">2x21</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：银行存款（或应收账款） 
50000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：租赁收入<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN>50000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">2x22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：银行存款（或应收账款）<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>75000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：租赁收入<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>75000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>49</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】沿用【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>46】,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租贷期届满时的处理——承租人行使购买权。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>分析:<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 270.15pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：银行存款 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>20000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 270.15pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：应收融资租赁款——租赁收款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l33 level1 lfo44; tab-stops: 424.9pt"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">3. </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>融资租赁变更的会计处理<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SUP>；</SUP><o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则规定.融资租赁发生变更且同时符合下列条件的，出租人应当将该变更作为一项单独租赁进行会计处理：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l53 level1 lfo48"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>该变更通过增加一项或多项租赁资产的使用权而扩大了租赁范围或延长了租赁期限；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l53 level1 lfo48; tab-stops: 42.55pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>增加的对价与租赁范围扩大部分或租赁期限延长部分的单独价格按该合同情况调整后的金额相当。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人就某套机器设备与出租人签订了一项为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁.构成融资租赁。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，承租人和出租人同意对原租赁进行修改，再増加</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">套机器设备用于租赁，租赁期也为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年。扩租的设备从第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年第二季度末时可供承租人使用。租赁总对价的增加额与新增的该套机器设备的当前出租市价扣减相关折扣相当。其中，折扣反映了出租人节约的成本，即若将同样设备租赁给新租户出租人会发生的成，.如营销成本等。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>分析：此情况下，该变更通过增加一项或多项租赁资产的使用权而扩大了租赁范围，增加的对价与租赁范围扩大部分的单独价格按该合同情况调整后的金额相当，应将该变更作为一项新的租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则规定，如果融资租赁的变更未作为一项单独租赁进行会计处理，且满足假如变更在租赁开始日生效，该租赁会被分类为经营租赁条件的，岀租人应当自租赁变更生效日开始将其作为一项新租赁进行会计处理，并以租赁变更生效日前的租赁投资净额作为租赁资产的账面价值。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>51</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人就某套机器设备与出租人签订了一项为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁，构成融资租赁。合同规定，每年末承租人向出租人支付租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，租赁期开始日，出租资产公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37908</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。按照公式</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>10000x(P/A,r,</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5)=37908</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(元)，计算得出租赁内含利率</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁收款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，未确认融资收益为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12092</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，承租人和出租人同意对原租赁进行修改，缩短租赁期限到第三年年末，每年支付租金时点不变，租金总额从</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元变更到</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>33000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。假设本例中不涉及未担保余值、担保余值、终止租赁罚款等。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：本例中，如果原租赁期限设定为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，在租赁开始日，租赁类别被分类为经营租赁，那么，在租赁变更生效日，即第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，出租人将租赁投资净额余额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31699</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37908+37908</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>-10000)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">作为该套机器设备的入账价值，并从第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初开始，作为一项新的经营租赁</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年租赁期，每年末收取租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>11500</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元)进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第二年年初会计分录如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：固定资产<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31699</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">应收融资租赁款——未确认融资收益 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>(12</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">092-37</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">908x10%)8301<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：应收融资租赁款——租赁收款额 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">(50000-10000)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">40000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">如果融资租赁的变更未作为一项单独租赁进行会计处理，且满足假如变更在租赁开始日生效，该租赁会被分类为融资租赁条件的，出租人应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一融工具确认和计量》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(2017)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第四十二条关于修改或重新议定合同的规定进行会计处理。即，修改或重新议定租赁合同，未导致应收融资租赁款终止确认,但导致未来现金流量发生变化的，应当重新计算该应收融资租赁款的账面余额，并将相关利得或损失计入当期损益。重新计算应收融资租赁款账面余额时，应当根据重新议定或修改的租赁合同现金流量按照应收融资租赁款的原折现率或按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>24</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一套期会计》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2017)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第二十三条规定重新计算的折现率(如适用)折现的现值确定。对于修改或重新议定租赁合同所产生的所有成本和费用，企业应当调整修改后的应收融资租赁款的账面价值，并在修改后应收融资租赁款的剩余期限内进行摊销。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>52</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人就某套机器设备与出租人签订了一坝为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁，构成融资租赁。合同规定，每年年末承租向出租人支付租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10000</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>元，租赁开始日租赁资产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37908</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，如例【51】，租赁内含利率</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%。在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，承租給人和出租人因为设备适用性等原因同意对原租赁进行修改，从第二年开始，每年支付租金变为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9500</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，租金总额从</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>50000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元变更到</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>48000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：如果此付款变更在租赁开始日生效，租赁类别仍被分类为融资租赁，那么，在租赁变更生效日——第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，按</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">原租赁內含利率重新计算租赁投资净额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>30114</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>［<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>9</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>500</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>.4</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）］，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">与原租赁投资总净额账面余额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31699</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的差额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1585</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（其中</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">应收融资租赁款</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">一租赁收款额”减少</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，“应收融资租赁款</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">一</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">未确认融资收益”减少</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>415</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元）计入当期损益。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第二年年初会计分录如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：租赁收入<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>1585<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>应收融资租赁款一未确认融资收益<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>415<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ae 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 35pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：应收融资租赁款一租赁收款额<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p><FONT 
size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（三）出租人对经营租赁的会计处理</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo49"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">1.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租金的处理<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期内各个期间，出租人应采用直线法或者其他系统合理的方法将经营租赁的租赁收款额确认为租金收人。如果其他系统合理的方法能够更好地反映因使用租赁资产所产生经济利益的消耗模式的，则出租人应采用该方法。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo49"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">2.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人对经营租赁提供激励措施<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>岀租人提供免租期的,整个租赁期内,按直线法或其他合理的方法进行分配，免租期内应当确认租金收人。出租人承担了承租人某些费用的，出租人应将该费用自租金收入总额中扣除,按扣除后的租金收入余额在租赁期内进行分配。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo49"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">3.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>初始直接费用<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人发生的与经非租赁有关的初始直接费用应当资本化至租赁标的资产的成本，在租赁期内按照与租金收人相同的确认基础分期计入当期损益。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo49; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">4.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>折旧和减值<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于经营租赁资产中的固定资产，岀租人应当采用类似资产的折旧政策计提折旧；对于其他经营租赁资产，应当恨据该资产适用的企业会计准则，采用系统合理的方法进行摊销</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">出租人应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一资产减值》的规定，确定经营租赁资产是否发生减值，并对已识别的减值损失进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo49; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">5.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>可变租赁付款额<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人取得的与经营租赁有关的可变租赁付款额，如果是与指数或比率挂钩的，应在租赁期开始日计入租赁收款额；除此之外的，应当在实际发生时计入当期损益。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo49; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">6.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>经营租赁的变更<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则规定，经营租赁发生变更的，出租人应自变更生效日开始，将其作为一项新的租赁进行会计处理，与变更前租赁有关的预收或应收租赁收款额视为新租赁的收款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-outline-level: 2; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_Toc72425525><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">九、特殊租赁业务的会计处理</SPAN></B></A><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（一</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">转租赁<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>转租情况下，原租赁合同和转租赁合同通常都是单独协商的，交易对手也是不同的企业、本准则要求转租出租人对原租赁合同和转租赁合同分別根据承租人和出租人会计处理要求，进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人在对转租赁进行分类时，转租出租人应基于原租赁中产生的使用权资产，而不是租赁资产（如作为租赁对象的不动产或设备）进行分类。原租赁资产不归转租出租人所有，原租赁资产也未计人其资产负债表。因，转租岀租人应基于其控制的资产（即使用权资产）进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>原租赁为短期租赁，且转租岀租人作为承租人已按照本准则采用简化会计处理方法的，应将转租赁分类为经营租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>53</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】甲企业（原租赁承租人）与乙企业（原租赁出租人）就</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米办公场所签订了一项为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁（原租赁）。在第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年年初，甲企业将该</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米办公场所转租给丙企业，期限为原租赁的剩余</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年时间（转租赁）。假设不考虑初始直接费用。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>分析：甲企业应基于原租赁形成的使用权资产对转租赁进行分类。本例中，转租赁的期限覆盖了原租赁的所有剩余期限，综合考虑其他因素，甲企业判断其实质上转移了与该项使用权资产有关的几乎全部风险和报酬，甲企业将该项转租赁分类为融资租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲企业的会计处理为：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">终止确认与原租赁相关且转给丙企业（转租承租人）的使用权资产，并确认转租赁投资净额；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">将使用权资产与转租赁投资净额之间的差额确认为损益；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（3）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在资产负债表中保留原租赁的租赁负债，该负债代表应付原租赁出租人的租赁付款额。在转租期间，中间出租人既要确认转租贷的租赁收益，也要确认原租赁的利息费用。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>54</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】甲企业（原租贷承租人）与乙企业（原租赁出租人）就</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方米办公场所签订了一项为期</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的租赁（原租赁）。在原租赁的租赁期开始日，甲企业将该</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">平方来办公场所转租给丙企业，期限为两年（转租赁）。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：甲企业基于原租赁形成的使用权资产对转租赁进行分类，考虑各种因素后，将其分类为经营租赁，签订转租赁时，中间出租人在其资产负债表中继续保留与原租赁相关的租赁负债和使用权资产。在转租期间，甲企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（1）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">确认使用权资产的折旧费用和租赁负债的利息；并</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（2）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">确认转租赁的租赁收入。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（二）生产商或经销商出租人的融资租赁会计处理<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>生产商或经销商通常为客户提供购买或租赁其产品或商品的选择。如果生产商或经销商出租其产品或商品构成融资租赁，则该交易产生的损益应相当于按照考虑适用的交易量或商业折扣后的正常售价直接销售标的资产所产生的损益。构成融资租赁的，生产商或经销商出租人在租赁期开始日应当按照租赁资产公允价值与租赁收款额按市场利率折现的现值两者孰低确认收入，并按照租赁资产账面价值扣除未担保余值的现值后的余额结转销售成本，收入和销售成本的差额作为销售损益。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>由于取得融资租赁所发生的成本主要与生产商或经销商赚取的销售利得相关，生产商或经销商出租人应当在租赁期开始日将其计入损益。即，与其他融资租赁出租人不同，生产商或经梢商出租人取得融资租赁所发生的成本不属于初始直接费用，不计入租赁投资净额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>55</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】甲公司是一家设备生产商，与乙公司（生产型企业）签订了一份租赁合同，向乙公司出租所生产的设备，合同主要条款如下：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（1）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁资产：设备</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>A</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（2）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁期：</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x21</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日，共</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（3）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租金支付：自</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>X19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年起每年年末支付年租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁合同规定的利率：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（年利率），与市场利率相同；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">该设备于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2700000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（6）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司取得该租赁发生的相关成本为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">该设备于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日交付乙公司，预计使用寿命为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，无残值；租赁期届满时，乙公司可以</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元购买该设备，预计租赁到期日该设备的公允价值不低于</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1500000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，乙公司对此金额提供担保；租赁期内该设备的保险、维修等费用均由乙公司自行承担。假设不考虑其他因素和各项税费影响。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>分析：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第一步，判断租赁类型。本例中租赁期满乙公司可以远低于租赁到期日租赁资产公允价值的金额购买租赁资产，甲公司认为其可以合理确定乙公司将行使购买选择权，综合考虑其他因素，与该项资产所有权有关的几乎所有风险和报酬已实质转移给乙公司，因此甲公司将该租赁认定为融资租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第二步，计算租赁期开始日租赁收款额按市场利率折现的现值，确定收入金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">租赁收款额=租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">期数+购买价格=</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">1000000</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">3+100=3000100</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">租赁收款额按市场利率折现的现值=</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">1000000</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">P/A</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">,5%,3）</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">+100x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/F,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">5%,3）=2723286</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 391.45pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">按照租赁资产公允价值与租赁收款额按市场利率折现的现值两者孰低的原则，确认收入为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2700000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第三步，计算租赁资产账面价值扣除未担保余值的现值后的余额，确定销售成本金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">俏售成本=账而价值-未担保余值的现值</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>=2000000</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>-</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0=<SPAN 
class=8><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">2000000（元）</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>第四步，会计分录：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日（租赁期开始日）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：应收融资租赁款——租赁收款额 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>3000100<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：营业收入 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>2700000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 60pt; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0; tab-stops: 330.5pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">应收融资租赁款——未实现融资收益</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>300100</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：营业成本 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN>2000000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：存货 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>2000000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>借：销售费用 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>5000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>贷：银行存款 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>5000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>由于甲公司在确定营业收入和租赁投资净额（即应收融资租赁款）时，是基于租赁资产的公允价值，因此，甲公司需要根据租赁收款额、未担保余值和租赁资产公允价值重新计算租赁内含利率。即，<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">1000000</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">x(P/A,r,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">3)</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">+100x(P/F,r,3)=2700000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">(元)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">r=5.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">4606%</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">=5.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">46%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">计算租赁期内各期分摊的融资收益如表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">所示。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>

<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>x19年12月31日会计分录：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><FONT 
size=3>借：应收融资租赁款——未实现融资收益 147436<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm auto 59pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm"><SPAN

size=3>贷：租赁收入 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>147436<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29pt"><SPAN
