size=3>借：银行存款<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN>1000000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm auto 59pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm"><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><FONT 
size=3>贷：应收融资租赁款——租贷收款额 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN>1000000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2x20年12月31日和2x21年12月31日会计分录略。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>56</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】甲公司是一家设备生产商，与乙公司(生产型企业)签订了一份租赁合，向乙公司出租所生产的设备，合同主要条款如下</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(1)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁资产：设备</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>A</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(2)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁期：</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">一</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x25</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月31日，共</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租全支付：自</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年起每年末支付年租金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>475000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(4)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁合同规定的利率：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(年利率)，与市场息率相同：</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(5)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">该设备于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2700000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，甲公司认为租赁到期时该设备余值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>72800</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，乙公司及其关联方未对余值提供担保；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(6)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司取得该程赁发生的相关成本为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(7)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">该设备于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日交付乙公司，预计使用寿命为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年；租赁期內该设备的保险、维修等费用均由乙公司自行承担：假设不考虑其他因素和各项税费影响。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 378.75pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>分析：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 368.05pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第一步，判断租赁类型。本例中租赁期与租赁资产预计使用寿命一致，另外租赁收款额的现值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2651600</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元(计算过程见后)，约为租赁资产公允价值的</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>98%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">综合考虑其他因素，甲公司认为与该项资产所有权有关的几乎所有风险和报酬已实质转移给乙公司，所以将该租赁认定为融资租赁。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 390.95pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>第二步，计算租赁期开始日租赁收款额按市场利率折现的现值，确定收入金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">租赁收款额=租金</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">期数</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">=475</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">000x7=3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">325000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">(元)<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">租赁收款额按市场利率折现的现值</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">=475000x(P/A,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">6%,7)=2651600</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">按照租赁资产公允价值与租赁收款额按市场利率折现的现值两者孰低的原则，确认收入为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2651600</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">注：</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">475</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">6%,7）=2651640</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元），为便于计算，作尾数调整，取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">2651600</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">元。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT

<P class=80

style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>注：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>**</SPAN>包括未实现融资收益的摊销和未担保余值产生的两部分。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>**</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">作尾数调整：<SPAN lang=EN-US>31075=475000-443925</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>443925=516725-728000</SPAN>（假定租赁资产余值估计一直未变。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>年<SPAN

<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm auto 30pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 25.35pt; TEXT-INDENT: -30pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><FONT

<P class=80

<P class=11

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x25</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=11

size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：应收融资租赁款——未实现融资收益<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>26931</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">应收融资租赁款</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">未担保余值 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4144</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：租赁收入 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31075</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: right 191.4pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">借：银行存款<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">475000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：应收融资租赁款——租赁收款额<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>475000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 331.4pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><o:p><FONT 
size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 331.4pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：融资租赁资产<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>72800</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 35pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.5; tab-stops: 205.55pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：应收融资租赁款——未担保余值<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>72800</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 305.6pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：银行存款<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>72800</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 7.0cm"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：融资租赁资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>72800</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>为吸引客户，生产商或经销商出租人有时以较低利率报价。使用该利率会导致出租人在租赁期开始日确认的收入偏髙。在这种情况下，生产商或经销商岀租人应当将销售利得限制为采用市场利率所能取得的销售利得。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（三）售后租回交易<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">若企业（卖方兼承租人）将资产转让给其他企业（买方兼出租人），并从买方兼出租人租回该项资产，则卖方兼承租人和买方兼出租人均应按照售后租回交易的规定进行会计处理：企业应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>14</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——收入》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2017）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">的规定，评估确定售后租回交易中的资产转让是否属于销售，并区别进行会计处理</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在标的资产的法定所有权转移给出租人并将资产租赁给承租人之前，承租人可能会先获得标的资产的法定所有权。但是，是否具有标的资产的法定所有权本身并非会计处理的决定性因素。如果承租人在资产转移给出租人之前已经取得对标的资产的控制，则该交易属于售后租回交易。然而，如果承租人未能在资产转移给出租人之前取得对标的资产的控制，那么即便承租人在资产转移给岀租人之前先获得标的资产的法定所有权，该交易也不属于售后租回交易。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l17 level1 lfo50"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">1.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>售后租回交易中的资产转让属于销售<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>卖方兼承租人应当按原资产账面价值中与租回获得的使用权有关的部分，计量售后租回所形成的使用权资产，并仅就转让至买方兼出租人的权利确认相关利得或损失。买方兼岀租人根据其他适用的《企业会计准则》对资产购买进行会计处理，并根据本准则对资产出租进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>如果销售对价的公允价值与资产的公允价值不同,或者出租人未按市场价格收取租金，企业应当进行以下调整：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l66 level1 lfo51; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>销售对价低于市场价格的款项作为预付租金进行会计处理!；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l66 level1 lfo51; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>销售对价高于市场价格的款项作为买方兼出租人向卖方兼承租人提供的额外融资进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>同时.承租人按照公允价值调整相关销售利得或损失，出租人按市场价格调整租金收入。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在进行上述调整时.企业应当按以下二者中较易确定者进行：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l29 level1 lfo52; tab-stops: 1.0cm"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>销售对价的公允价值与资产的公允价值的差异；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l29 level1 lfo52; tab-stops: 1.0cm"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>合同付款额的现值与按市场租金计算的付款额的现值的差异。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l17 level1 lfo50; tab-stops: 1.0cm"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">2.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>售后租回交易中的资产转让不属于销售<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">卖方兼承租人不终止确认所转让的资产，而应当将收到的现金作为金融负债，并按照〈企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一金融工具确认和计量〉</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(2017)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">进行会计处理。买方兼岀租人不确认被转让资产，而应当将支付的现金作为金融资产，并按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一融工具确认和计量》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(2017)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l17 level1 lfo50; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">3.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>售后租回交易示例<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo53"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>售后租回交易中的资产转让不属于销售。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>57</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司(卖方兼承租人)以货币资金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>24000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的价格向乙公司(买方兼出租人)出售一栋建筑物，交易前该建筑物的账面原值是</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>24000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，累计折旧是</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。与此同时，甲公司与乙公司签订了合同，取得了该建筑物</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>18</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的使用权(全部剩余使用年限为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>40</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年)，年租金为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，于每年年末支付,租赁期满时，甲公司将以</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元购买该建筑物。根据交易的条款和条件，甲公司转让建筑物不满足《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>14</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号收入》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>(2017)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">中关于销售成立的条件。假设不考虑初始直接费用和各项税费的影响。该建筑物在销售当日的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>36000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 289.3pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>分析：在租赁期开始日，甲公司对该交易的会计处理如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：货币资金<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>24000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">贷：长期应付款<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">24000000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 289.3pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在租赁期开始日，乙公司对该交易的会计处理如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：长期应收款<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>24000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">贷：货币资金<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">24000000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（2）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">售后租回交易中的资产转让属于销售。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>58</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】甲公司（卖方兼承租人）以货币资金</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>40000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元的价格向乙公司（买方兼出租人）出售一栋建筑物，交易前该建筑物的账面原值是</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>24000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，累计折旧是</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。与此同时，甲公司与乙公司签订了合同，取得了该建筑物</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>18</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年的使用权（全部剩余使用年限为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>40</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年），年租金为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2400000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，于每年年末支付。根据交易的条款和条件，甲公司转让建筑物符合《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>14</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——收入》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2017）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">中关于销售成立的条件。假设不考虑初始直接费用和各项税费的影响。该建筑物在销售当日的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>36000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">分析：由于该建筑物的销售对价并非公允价值，甲公司和乙公司分别进行了调整，以按照公允价值计量销售收益和租赁应收款。超额售价</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>40000000-36000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">作为乙公司向甲公司提供的额外融资进行确认。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=80 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">甲、乙公司均确定租赁内含年利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">4.5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">。年付款额现值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">29183980</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">元（年付款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">2400000,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">共</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">18</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">期，按每年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">4.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">5%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">进行折现），其中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">4000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">元与额外融资相关，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">25183980</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">元与租赁相关</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">分别对应年付款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">328948</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">元和</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">2071052</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">元），具体计算过程如下：年付款额现值=</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">2400000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">4.5%,18）=29183980</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元），额外融资年付款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">=4000000/29183980</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">x2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">400000=328948</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元），租赁相关年付款额</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">=2400000</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">-328</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">948=2071052</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 375.75pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁期开始日，甲公司对该交易的会计处理如下<SUP>：<o:p></o:p></SUP></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 375.75pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第一步，按与租回获得的使用以部分占该建筑物的原账面金额的比例计算售后租回所形成的使用权资产<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 375.75pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"></SPAN></SPAN></FONT><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">使用权资产=</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（24000000</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">-4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">000000）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（注</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">1）</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">*</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">25183980</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（注</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">2）</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">/</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">36000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（注</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">3））=13991100</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">（元）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 22pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt">注</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>：</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt">该建筑的的账面价值；<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 22pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt">注</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US

<P class=11

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2400000</SPAN><SPAN

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>328948</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=11

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元而收到的款项；</SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT

<P class=80

<P class=33

style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（一）承租人的列报和披露<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">资产负债表<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人应当在资产负债表中单独列示使用权资产和租赁负债。其中，租赁负债通常分别非流动负债和一年内到期的非流动负债（即，资产负债表日后</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月内租赁负债预期减少的金额）列示。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>59】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">沿用【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>36</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>】</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在租赁开始日，甲公司确认的租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>43300</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，租赁负债将按以下方法进行后续计量（如表</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">所示）：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 342.2pt"><SPAN

      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>18</SPAN></B><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>600</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 20.6pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 74.8pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=100>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>930</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 20.6pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 85.65pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=114>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>10000</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 20.6pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 97.15pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=130>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>9530</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR 
  style="HEIGHT: 22.35pt; mso-yfti-irow: 6; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 22.35pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 46.15pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=62>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>5</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 22.35pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 95.05pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=127>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>9530</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 22.35pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 74.8pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=100>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>470</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 22.35pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 85.65pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=114>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>10000</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 22.35pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 97.15pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-left-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=130>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B><SPAN 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>—</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE></DIV>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p><FONT 
size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 377.3pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在第一年年末，甲公司约租赁负债为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>35465</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，其中，应列示为非流动负债的金额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>27238</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，应列示为一年内到期的非流动负债的全额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8227</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元（即</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>35465-27238）,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">该金额是资产负债表日后</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月内租赁负债预期减少的金额。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">利润表<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当在利润表中分别列示租赁负债的利息费用与使用权资产的折旧费用。其中，租赁负债的利息费用在财务费用项目列示。对于金融企业，财务报表格式中没有财务费用项目，因此使用权资产的折旧费用和利息费用可以在“业务及管理费用”列示,并在附注中进一步披露。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&#12539;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">现金流量表<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当在现金流量表中按照如下方式列示:<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l39 level1 lfo54; tab-stops: 1.0cm"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>偿还租赁负债本金和利息所支付的现金，应当计入筹资活动现金流出；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l39 level1 lfo54; tab-stops: 1.0cm"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>按照本准则有关规定对短期租赁和低价值资产租赁进行简化处理的，支付的相关付款额，应当计入经营活动现金流出；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l39 level1 lfo54; tab-stops: 1.0cm"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>支付的未纳入租赁负债计量的可变租赁付款额，应当计入经营活动现金流出。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>4.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人的披露<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当在财务报表附注中披露有关租赁活动的定性和定址信息，以便财务报表使用者评估租赁活动对承租人的财务状况、经营成果和现金流量的影响。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当在财务报表的单独附注或单独章节中披露其作为承租人的信息，但无需重复已在财务报表其他部分列报或披露的信息,只需要在租赁的相关附注中通过交叉索引的方式体现该信息。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当在财务报表附注中披露与租赁有关的下列信息：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>各类使用权资产的期初余额、本期增加额、期末余额以及累计折旧额和减值金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁负债的利息费用。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>有关简化处理方法的披露。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人按照本准则有关规定对短期租赁和低价值资产租赁进行简化处理的，应当披瞬这一事实，并且，应当披露计入当期损益的短期租赁费用和低价值资产租赁费用。其中，短期租赁费用无需包含租赁期在</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月以内的租赁相关费用，低价值资产租赁费用不应包含已包括在上述短期租赁费用中的低价值资产短期租赁费用。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>若承租人在报告期末承诺的短期租赁组合与上述披露的短期租赁费用所对应的短期租赁组合不同，则承租人应当披露简化处理的短期租赁的租赁承诺金额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>计人当期损益的未纳入租赁负债计量的可变租赁付款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(5)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>转租使用权资产取得的收入。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(6)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>与租赁相关的总现金流岀。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(7)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>售后租回交易产生的相关损益。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-list: l42 level1 lfo55; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(8)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——金融工具列报》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>(</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2017)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">应当披露的有关租赁负债的信息.包括单独披露租赁负债的到期期限分析、对相关流动性风险的管理等。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当以列表格式披露上述信息，其他格式更为适当的除外，值得注意的是，承租人披露的金额应包含已在当期计入其他资产账面价值的成本。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>此外，承租人应当根据理解财务报表的需要，披露有关租赁活动的其他定性和定量信息：此类信息包括：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l27 level1 lfo56; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁活动的性质。例如，租入资产的类别及数量、租赁期、是否存在续租选择权等租赁基本情况信息。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l27 level1 lfo56; tab-stops: 35.45pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>未纳人租赁负债计量的未来潜在现金流出。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>未纳入租赁负债计量的未来潜在现金流岀主要来源于下列风险敞口：一是可变租赁付款额，二是续租选择权与终止租赁选择权,三是担保余值，四是承租人已承诺但尚未开始的租赁。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l15 level1 lfo57"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>①</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>可变租赁付款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人可能需要根据具体情况披露与可变租赁付款额有关的额外信息，以帮助财务报表使用者进行评估。例如：承租人使用可变租赁付款额的原因，以及使用此类付款额的普遍性；可变租赁付款额相对于固定付款额的大小；可变租赁付款额所依据的主要变量,以及付款额预期将如何随主要变量变化而变动；可变租赁付款额的其他经营及财务影响。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>60</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】零售商甲公司租入了大量零售店铺，其中许多租赁包含与店铺销售额挂钩的可变付款额条款。甲公司的政策规定，可变租赁付款额条款的使用情形以及所有租赁商洽均须集中审批。租赁付款额受到集中监督。甲公司认为，关于可变租赁付款额的信息对财务报表使用者有重大意义，且无法从财务报表的其他部分获得。此外，甲公司认为，下列信息对财务报表使用者也有重大意义：甲公司就可变租赁付款额所用的不同类型的合同条款，这些条款对其财务状况的影响，以及可变租赁付款额对销售额变化的敏感度等，这些信息与向甲公司的高级管理层报告时所用的有关可变租赁付款额的信息类似。因此，甲公司在其财务报表附注中对租赁进行如下披露：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">本集团的许多房地产租赁包含与租入店铺的销售额挂钩的可变租赁付款额条款。在可能的情况下，本集团使用该等条款的目的是将租赁的付款额与产生较多现金流的店铺相匹配。对于单独的店铺，最高可有</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>100%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">的付款额是基于可变租赁付款额的，并且，用于确定付款额的销售额比例范围较大。在某些情况下，可变租赁付款额条款还包含年度付款额的下限或上限。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x07</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年度，租赁付款额及条款汇总如表</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">所示。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
表</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>1153000</SPAN></B><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 18.85pt; mso-yfti-irow: 2; mso-height-rule: exactly">
    <TD

<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p><FONT 
size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">若本集团全部店铺的销售额增长</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁付款总额预期将增长约</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0.6%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0.7%</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">若木集团全部店铺的销售额增长</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁付款总额预期将增长约</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">至</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2.8%<SUB>0</SUB></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>61】零</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">售商甲公司租入了大量零售店铺。这些租贷包含差异较大的可变租赁付款额条款。租赁条款由当地管理层商洽和监督。甲公司认为，关于可变租赁付款额的信息对财务报表使用者有重大意义，且无法从财务报表的其他部分获得。并且，甲公司认为，关于如何管理房地产租赁组合的信息对财务报表使用者有重大意义。此外，甲公司认为，关于以后年度的可变租赁付款额预计水平的信息（与向甲公司的高级管理层报告时所用的信息类似）对财务报表使用者也有重大意义。因此，甲公司在其财务报表附注中对租赁进行如下披露：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本集团的许多房地产租赁包含可变租赁付款额条款。当地管理层对店铺的利润率负责，因此，租赁条款由当地管理层商洽确定，付款额条款类型多样。使用可变租赁付款额条款有多种原因，包括最小化新开店固定成本额、管理利润率以及保持经营灵活性等。本集团的可变程赁付额条款差异较大：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>——大部分可变租赁付款额条款是基于店铺销售额的一定比例；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">——基于可变条款的付款额占单个房地产租赁付款总额的比例为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>0-20%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">；<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>——部分可变租赁付款额条款包含下限或上限条款。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>使用可变租赁付款额条款的总体财务影响是：店铺的销售额越高，租金成本越高。这将有利于本集团的利润管理。预计未来几年可变租赁付款额相关的租赁费用占店铺销售额的比例将保持类似水平。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l15 level1 lfo57; tab-stops: 42.55pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>②</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>续租选择权与终止租赁选拯权。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>根据具体情况，承租人可能需要披露与续租选择权或终止租赁选择权有关的额外信息，以帮助财务报表使用者进行评估。例如：承租人使用续租选择权或终止选择权的原因，以及此类选择权的普遍性；选择权期间租金相对于租赁付款额的大小；行使未纳人租赁负债计量的选择权的普遍性;此类选择权的其他经营及财务影响。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>62</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司有大量设备租赁，这些租赁的条款和条件差异较大。租赁条款由当地管理层商洽和监督。甲公司认为，如何对终止租赁选择权和续租选择权的使用进行管理的信息对财务报表使用者有重大意义，且无法从财务报表的其他部分获得。此外，甲公司认为，下列信息对财务报表使用者也有重大意义：重新评估上述选择权的财务影响，以及在其短期租赁组合中，包含无罚金年度解约条款的租赁所占的比例。因此，甲公司在其财务报表附注中对租赁进行如下披露：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本集团有大量设备租赁包含续租选择权和终止租赁选择权。当地管理层负责管理其租赁。因此，租赁条款是以逐项租赁为基础进行商洽的，并且这些租赁的条款和条件差异较大。在可能的情况下，租赁会使用续租选择权和终止租赁选择权条款，以便当地管理层在取得所需设备与履行客户合同的一致性方面拥有更大的灵活性。本集团所用的租赁具体条款和条件不尽相同。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>大部分续租选择权和终止租赁选择权仅可由本集团行使，而非由相应的出租人行使。若本集团不能合理确定将行使续租选择权，则续租期间的相关付款额不纳入租赁负债的计量。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x07</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，因续租选择权或终止租赁选择权的评估结果或实际行使情况发生变化导致租赁期变化，本集团确认的租赁负债增加</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>489000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">此外，本集团有大量租赁安排包含无罚金的年度解约条款。这些租赁被分类为短期租赁，且未包含在租赁负债中。本集团在</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x07</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年确认的短期租赁费用为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>30000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，其中包含年度解约条款的租赁发生的租赁赍用为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>27000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>63</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】承租人甲公司有大量大型设备租赁，这些租赁包含可由甲公司行使的续租选择权。甲公司的政策是,在可能的惜况下使用续租选择权，从而使得已承诺的大型设备的租赁期与相关客户合同的初始合同期限一数.同时保留管理大型设备以及在不同合同间重新分配资产的灵活性。甲公司认为，关于续租选择权的信息对财务报表使用者有重大意义，且无法从财务报表的其他部分获得。此外，甲公司认为，下列信息对财务报表使用者也有重大意义：未纳入租赁负债计量的未来租赁付款额的潜在风险敞口，以及过去已行使的续租选择权所占比例。这与向甲公司的高级管理层报告时所用的有关续租选择钗的信息类似。因此，甲公司在其财务报表附注中对租赁进行如下披露：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">本集团的许多大型设备租赁包含续租选择权。这些条款可最大化合同管理的灵活性。在许多情况下，这些条款并未纳入租赁负债的计量，因为本集团无法合理确定是否将行使这些选择权。表</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">汇总了与续租选择权可行权之后期间相关的潜在未来付款额：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=ad 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
表10<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>

      <P class=ae

      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>69</SPAN></B><SPAN

  <TR style="HEIGHT: 18.85pt; mso-yfti-irow: 3; mso-height-rule: exactly">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 18.85pt; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 56.6pt; BACKGROUND: white; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0.5pt; BORDER-LEFT: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 0.5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt" 
    width=75>
      <P class=ae 
      style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt">分部</SPAN><B><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt'>C</SPAN></B><SPAN
