<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p><FONT 
size=3>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l56 level1 lfo58"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>③</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>担保余值。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>根据具体情况，承租人可能需要披露与担保余值有关的额外信息，以帮助财务报表使用者进行评估。例如，承租人提供担保余值的原因，以及此类条款的普遍性；承租人担保余值风险敞口的相对大小；被担保的标的资产的性质；其他经营及财务影响。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l28 level1 lfo59; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>租赁导致的限制或承诺。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>根据具体情况，承租人可能需要披露与租赁导致的限制或承诺有关的额外信息，以帮助财务报表使用者进行评估。例如，租赁合同中关于承租人维持特定财务比率的条款。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l28 level1 lfo59; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>售后租回交易。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>根据具体情况，承租人可能需要披露与售后租回有关的额外信息，以帮助财务报表使用者进行评估。例如：承租人进行售后租回交易的原因，以及此类交易的普遍性；各项售后租回交易的主要条款与条件；未纳入租赁负债计量的付款额；售后租回交易对当期现金流量的影响。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l28 level1 lfo59; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(5)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>其他相关信息。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>在确定有关租赁活动的上述其他定性和定量信息是否属于必要信息时，承租人应考虑以下两个方面：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l32 level1 lfo60; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>①</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>该信息是否与财务报表使用者相关。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当仅在预期其他定性和定量信息与财务报表使用者相关的情况下，才提供这些信息。如果这些信息可帮助财务报表使用者了解以下事项，则可能属于此情形：一是租赁带来的灵活性，租赁可提供一定的灵活性，例如，承租人可通过行使终止选择权或以有利的条款和条件进行续租的方式降低风险敞口；二是租赁施加的限制，租赁可施加多种限制，例如，要求承租人维持特定的财务比率；三是报表信息对关键变量的敏感性，例如，报表信息可能对未来可变租赁付款额较为敏感；四是租赁产生的其他风险敞口；五是偏离行业惯例，例如，此类偏离可能包括一些罕见或特殊的租赁条款与条件，从而影响承租人的租赁组合。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l32 level1 lfo60; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>②</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>该信息是否可以从财务报表主表列报或附注中披露的信息直观得出。承租人无需重复披露已在财务拒表其他部分列报或披露的信息。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>(二)出租人的列报和披霞<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>岀租人应当根据资产的性质，在资产负债表中列示经营租赁资产。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人应当在财务报表附注中披露有关租赁活动的定性和定量信息，以便财务报表使用者评估租赁活动对岀租人的财务状况、经营成果和现金流量的影响。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">与融资租赁有关的信息<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>岀租人应当在附注中披露与融资租赁有关的下列信息:<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l65 level1 lfo61; tab-stops: 81.75pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>销售损益(生产商或经销商出租人)、租赁投资净额的融资收益以及与未纳入租赁投资净额的可变租赁付款额相关的收入；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>岀租人应当以列表形式按露上述信息，其他形式更为适当的除外。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l65 level1 lfo61; tab-stops: 82.25pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>资产负债表日后连续五个会计年度每年将收到的未折现租赁收款额，以及剩余年度将收到的未折现租赁收款额总额；不足五个会计年度的，披露资产负债表日后连续每年将收到的未折现租赁收款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 355.7pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人应进行上述到期分析，并对融资租赁投资净额账面金额的重大变动提供定性和定量说明，以使财务报表使用者能够更准确地预测未来的租赁现金流量流动性风险。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l65 level1 lfo61; tab-stops: 80.7pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3) </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>未折现租赁收款额与租赁投资净额的调节表。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>调节表应说明与租赁应收款相关的未实现融资收益、未担保余值的现值。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l21 level1 lfo62"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">2.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>与经营租赁有关的信息<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>岀租人应当在附注中披露与经营租赁有关的下列信息：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l69 level1 lfo63"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁收入，并单独披露与未纳人租赁收款额计量的可变租赁付款额相关的收入。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>与融资租赁出租人披露信息类似，岀租人应当以列表形式披需上述信息，其他形式更为适当的除外。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l69 level1 lfo63; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">将经营租赁固定资产与岀租人持有自用的固定资产分开,并按经营租赁固定资产的类别提供《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一固定资产》要求披需的信息。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人对经营租赁下租赁的资产采用与其在其他经营活动中持有和使用的自有资产相似的方式进行会计处理。然而，租赁资产与自有资产通常被用于不同的目的，即租赁资产产生租赁收入，而不是对出租人的其他经营活动作出贡献。因此，将出租人持有和使用的自有资产与产生租赁收入的租赁资产分开披露，有利于财务报表使用者了解更多信息。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l69 level1 lfo63; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>资产负债表日后连续五个会计年度每年将收到的未折现租赁收款额，以及剩余年度将收到的未折现租赁收款总额。不足五个会计年度的，披露资产负债表日后连续每年将收到的未折现租赁收款额。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>与融资租赁披露类似，上述到期分析将使财务报表使用者能够更准确地预测未来的租赁现金流量流动性风险。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l21 level1 lfo62"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">3.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>其他信息<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>此外，出租人应当根据理解财务报表的需要，披露有关租赁活动的其他定性和定量信息。此类信息包括：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo64; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>租赁活动的性质。例如，租出资产的类别及数量、租赁期、是否存在续租选择权等租赁基本情况信息。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo64"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对其在租赁资产中保留的权利进行风险管理的情况。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>出租人应当披露其如何对其在租赁资产中保留的权利进行风险管理管理的策略,包括出租人降低风险的方式。该等方式可包括回购协议、担保余值条款或因超出规定限制使用资产而支付的可变租赁付款额等。如租赁设备和车辆的市场价值的下降幅度超过出租人在为租赁定价时的预计幅度，则对该项租赁的收益能力产生不利影响。租赁期结束时租赁资产余値的不确定性住往是出租人面临的重要风险。披餌有关出资人如何对租赁资产中保阳的权利进行管理，有利于财务报表使用者了解更多出租人相关风管理信息。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（3）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">其他相关信息。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l21 level1 lfo62"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">4.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>转租赁的列报<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">原租赁以及转租同-标的资产形成的资产和负债所产生的风险敞口不同于由于单一租赁应收款净额或租赁负债所产生的风险敞口，因此，企业不得以净额为基础对转租赁进行列报。除非满足《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>37</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——金融工具列报》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2017）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">第二十八条关于金融资产负债抵销的规定，转租出租人不得抵销由于原租赁以及转租同一租赁资产而形成的资产和负债，以及与原租赁以及转租同一租赁资产相关的租赁收益和租赁费用。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 20.1pt; mso-outline-level: 2; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_Toc72425527><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>十一、衔接规定</FONT></SPAN></B></A><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">(</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">一<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>)</SPAN></SPAN></B><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">首次执行日<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>本准则所述的首次执行日，是指企业首次采用本准则的年度报告期间的开始日。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 24pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; tab-stops: 76.3pt"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（二）租赁定义的实务豁免<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对于首次执行日前已存在的合同，企业在首次执行日可以选择不重新评估其是否为租赁或者包含租赁。即，企业可以仅对之前根据原租赁准则识别为租赁的合同采用本准则；对之前按原租赁准则未识别为包含租赁的合同不采用本准则。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>选择不重新评估的，企业应当在财务报表附注中披露这一事实，并一致应用于前述所有合同。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 24pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; tab-stops: 76.3pt"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（三）承租人衔接规定及示例<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人可以选择的衔接会计处理<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人应当选择下列方法之一对租赁进行衔接会计处理，并一致应用于其作为承租人的所有租赁：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo65; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>28</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一计政瓶会计估计变更和差错更正》的规定采用追溯调整法处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo65; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>根据首次执行本准则的累积影响数，调整首次执行本准则当年年初留存收益及财务报表其他相关项目金额，不调整可比期间信息(以下简称“简化的追溯调整法”)。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&#12539;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">简化的追溯调整法下具体衔接规定<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l26 level1 lfo66"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于首次执行日前的融资租赁，承租人在首次执行日应当按照融资租入资产和应付融张租赁款的原账而价值,分别</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>计量使用</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">权资产和租赁负债。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l26 level1 lfo66; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对于首次执行日前的经营租赁,承租人在首次执行日应当根据剩余租赁付款额按首次执行日承租人増录借款利率折现的现值计量租赁负债，并根据每项租赁选择按照下列两者之一计量使用权资产：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l62 level1 lfo67; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>①</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>假设自租窝期开始日即采用本准则的帐面价值(采用首次执行日的承租人増量借款利率作为折现率);<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l62 level1 lfo67; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore"><FONT face=宋体>②</FONT><SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>与租赁负债相等的金额，并根据预付租金进行必要调整。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l26 level1 lfo66; tab-stops: 49.65pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">在首次执行日，承租人应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——资产减值〉的规定，对使用权资产进行减值测试并进行相应会计处理，<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l24 level1 lfo68"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">3.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>简化的追溯调整法下对于经营租赁的额外可选简化处理<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 17.7pt; mso-char-indent-count: 1.77"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对于首次执行日前的经营租赁，可根据每项租赁采用下列一项或多项简化处理：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l59 level1 lfo69; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">将于首次执行日后</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月内执行完毕的租赁，可作为短期租赁处理。即，以本准则第三十二条所述的短期租赁处理方式对此类租赁进行会计处理，并在包含首次执行日的年度报告期间披露的短期租赁费用中涵盖与此类租赁有关的费用。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l59 level1 lfo69; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>计量租赁负债时，具有相似特征的租赁可采用同一折现率;使用权资产的计量可不包含初始直接费用。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l59 level1 lfo69; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>存在续租选择权或终止租赁选择权的，承租人可根据首次执行日前选择权的实际行使及其他最新情况确定租赁期，无需对首次执行日前各期间是否合理确定行使续租选择权或终止租赁选择权进行估计。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l59 level1 lfo69; tab-stops: 21.3pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">作为使用权资产减值测试的替代，承租人可根据《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——或有事项》评估包含租赁的合同在首次执行日前是否是亏损合同,并根据首次执行</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>前计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">入资产负债表的亏损准备金额调整使用权资产。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">值得注意的是,该方法只是对使用权减值测试的替代，该方祛</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>下计提</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">的使用权资产减值准务后续期间仍不得转回。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>（5）首次执行本准则当年年初之前发生租赁变更的，承租人无需按照本准则关于租赁变更的规定进行追溯调幣，而息根据租赁变更的最终安排，按照本准则进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l24 level1 lfo68"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-language: EN-US'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">4.<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>其他衔接规定<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>首次执行日前的经营租赁中，租赁资产属于低价值资产且根据本准则选择不确认使用权资产和租赁负债的，承租人无需对该经营租赁按照衔接规定进行调整，应当自首次执行日起按照本准则进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>母公司执行本准则、但子公司尚未执行本准则的，母公司在编制合并财务报表时，应当按照本准则规定调整子公司的财务报表。母公司尚未执行本准则、而子公司已执行本准则的，母公司在编制合并财务报表时，可以将子公司的财务报表按照母公司的会计政策进行调整后合并，也可以将子公司按照本准则编制的财务报表直接合并，母公司将子公司按照本准则编制的财务报表直接合并的，应当在合并财务报表中披露该事实，并且对母公司和子公司的会计政策及其他相关信息分别进行披露。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例</SPAN><B><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>64</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">】甲公司于</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>X19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日（假设为首次执行日）存在下列原租赁准则下的尚未执行完毕的租赁合同，其中第一项为融资租赁，其余各项为经营租赁。具体情况如下（下述合同均不涉及租赁激励，也不考虑相关税费影响）：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（1）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x16</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日（亦为该租</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>赁</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">的租赁期开始日）订立了一项</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年期机器租赁，约定自</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x16</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日起，每</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月于月末支付租金</SPAN><SPAN

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日），并可选择在租赁期满时延长一次</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年租赁期，租金不变，该选择最迟须在租赁到期前</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月书面通知出租人，否则视为放弃该选择权，该设备于租赁期开始日的预计剩余使用年限为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，未发生租赁初始直接费用。于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x18</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>30</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日，甲公司书面通知出租人选择延长，延长的租赁期届满时归还设备（以下简称“租赁</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>E”</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>）</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>分析：甲公司的衔接处理如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x19</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日（即首次执行日），甲公司选择不重新评估该此前已存在的合同是否为租赁或者是否包含租赁，并将此方法一致应用于所有合同，因此仅对上述在原租赁准则下识别为租赁的合同采用本准则衔接规定。此外，甲公司对上述租赁合同采用简化的追溯调整法进行衔接会计处理，并对其中的经营租赁根据每项租赁选择使用权资产计量方法和采用相关简化处理，具体如下：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>融资租入固定资产——累计折旧——机器<SPAN

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>9%,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">选择假设自租赁期开始日即采用本准则的账面价值（采用首次执行日的承租人增量借款利率</SPAN><SPAN

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%,</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=11

<P class=11

</SPAN>3000000<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">假设上述情况下，甲公司选择按与租赁负债相等的金额并根据预付租金进行调整的方法计量使用权资产，则使用权资产账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2759100</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元(即与租赁负债相等)。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo65; tab-stops: 49.65pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(3)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于租赁</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>C,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司确定适用于该租赁的首次执行日承租人增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(与</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>2x18</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">月</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">日确定亏损合同准备金额折现率相等)，选择按与租赁负债相等的金额并根据预付租金进行必要调整的方法计量使用权资产，采用前述简化处理第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">条，即作为使用权资产减值测试的替代，根据首次执行日前亏损准条金额调整使用权资产，不采用其他简化处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">于首次执行日:租赁负债=剩余租赁付款额按首次执行日承租人增量借款利率折现的现值=</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>500000+500</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>000x(P/A,</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>10%,1)=954545</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(元)<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">使用权资产原值=租赁负债</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>=954545</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(元)<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">使用权资产减值准备=相关预计负债金额</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>=694215</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">(元)<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>会计分录如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 323.45pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：使用权资产——原值——生产线<SPAN

</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>954545</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=80

size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: MingLiU">预计负债<SPAN

</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">694215<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11

<P class=11

<P class=11

size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁负债——租赁付款额——生产线<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>1000000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo65; tab-stops: 42.55pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(4)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于租赁</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>D,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司仅采用前述简化处理第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3(1)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">条，不采用其他简化处理，即将于首次执行日后</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">个月内执行完毕的租赁，作为短期租赁处理，并按照租赁资产类别将租赁付款额在租赁期内按直线法计入当期损益，不确认使用权资产和租赁负债，因此于首次执行日无需进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo65; tab-stops: 1.0cm"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(5)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于汽车租赁，甲公司计量租赁负债时，认为公务车租赁和轿车租赁具有相似特征，采用前述简化处理第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3(2)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">条，即针对各公务车租赁和轿车租赁适用的承租人増量借款利率采用同一</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>折</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">现率（确定适用于该情况的承租人增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8%）,</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于使用权资产，选择按与租任负债相等的金额并根据预付租金进行必要调整的方法计量，不采用其他简化处理。同时，甲公司认为上述各项汽车租贷符合组合处理的条件，因此就该组合进行相关会计处理。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">于首次执行日：汽车诅赁血债=公务车和轿车剩余租赁付款额之和按首次拭行日承租人增量借款利率折现的现值=</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（35000+25000）</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">%，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2）=106998</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（元）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">汽车租赁使用权资产原值=租赁负债=</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>106998</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（元）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>会计分录如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11

<P class=11

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>租赁负债——未确认融资费用——汽车租赁

<P class=11

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>120000</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=11

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（6）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于租赁</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>E.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">甲公司采用前述简化处理第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>3（3）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">条，即根据首次执行前选择权的实际行使情况确定租赁期，因此剩余租赁期为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">年，剩余租赁付款额为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>200000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">元，确定适用于该租赁的首次执行日承租人增量借款利率为</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8%</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Arial Unicode MS"'>；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于使用权资产，选择按与租赁负债相等的金额并根据预付租金进行必要调整的方法计量，不釆用其他简化处理：<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">于首次执行日：租赁负债=剰余租任付款额按首次执行日承租人增量借款利率折现的现值</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">=</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>100000x</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US'>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>P/A,</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>8%,2）=178330</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（元）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">使用权资产原值=租赁负债=</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>178330</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">（元）<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT size=3>会计分录如下：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">借：使用权资产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-language: EN-US">——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">原值——设备租赁<SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>178330</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">租赁负债——未确认融资费用——设备租赁<SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>21670<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 40pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">贷：租赁负债——租赁付款额——设备租赁</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>200000</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 2.0cm"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（四）<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN>出租人衔接规定<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>除下而所述情形外，出租人无需对作为出租人的租赁按照衔接规定进行调整，而应当自首次执行日起按照本准则进行会计处理：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对于首次执行日前划分为经营租赁且在首次执行日后仍继续的转租赁，转租岀租人在首次执行日应当基于原租赁和转租赁的剩余合同期限和条款进行重新评估，并按照本准则的规定进行分类。按照本准则重分类为融资租赁的，应当将其作为一项新的融资租赁进行会计处理。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 49.65pt"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（五）<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN>之前确认的有关企业合并的金额<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">承租人如果之前根据《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>20</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号一业合<SPAN 
style="COLOR: #564c4c">并》，</SPAN>对作为企业合并一部分购买的经营租赁的有利或不利条款确认了资产或负债，则应当终止确认该资产或负债，并相应调整首次执行日的使用权资产的账面金额。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24.1pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; tab-stops: 2.0cm"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（六）<SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN>售后租回交易的衔接规定<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">对于首次执行日前已存在的售后租回交易，企业在首次执行日不重新评估资产转让是否满足《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>14</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">号——收人》</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'>（2017）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">作为销售进行会计处理的规定。<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>对于首次执行日前应当作为销售和融资租赁进行会计处理的售后租回交易，卖方（承租人）应当按照与首次执行日存在的其他融资租赁相同的方法对租回进行会计处理，并继续在租赁期内摊销相关递延收益或损失。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>対于首次执行日前应当作为销售和经营租赁进行会计处理的售后租回交易，卖方（承租人）应当按照与首次执行日存在的其他经营租赁相同的方法对租回进行会计处理，并根据首次执行日前计入资产负债表的相关递延收益或损失调整使用权资产。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=33 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 24pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%">（七）披露要求<o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人釆用本准则第六十三条规定的简化处理方法的，应当在财务报表附注中披露所采用的简化处理方法以及在合理可能的范围内对采用每项简化处理方法的估计影响所作的定性分析。<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>承租人选择简化的追溯调整法对租赁进行衔接会计处理的，还应当在首次执行日披露以下信息：<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l36 level1 lfo70"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(1)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>首次执行日计人资产负债表的租赁负债所采用承租人增量借款利率的加权平均值；<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=11 
style="BACKGROUND: none transparent scroll repeat 0% 0%; MARGIN: auto 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-list: l36 level1 lfo70; tab-stops: 42.55pt"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Trebuchet MS",sans-serif; COLOR: black; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Trebuchet MS"'><SPAN 
style="mso-list: Ignore">(2)<SPAN 
style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3>首次执行日前一年度报告期末披露的重大经营租赁的尚未支付的最低租赁付款额按首次执行日承租人增量借款利率折现的现值.与计人首次执行日资产负债表的租赁负债的差额。</FONT><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
